select SYSDATE
from dual;

select to_char(sysdate,'day')
from dual;

select to_char(sysdate,'month'), to_char(sysdate,'year')
from dual;

select to_char(sysdate,'am')
from dual;

select next_day(sysdate,'friday')
from dual;

select round(sysdate,'month')
from dual;

select trunc(sysdate,'month')
from dual;

select round(sysdate,'year')
from dual;

select trunc(sysdate,'year')
from dual;

select to_char(sysdate+3,'day')
from dual;

create table Emp1(empno number, Name varchar2(20), doj date);

insert into Emp1 values(1,'Max','13-Dec-2021');
insert into Emp1 values(2,'Kimi','4-Feb-2022');
insert into Emp1 values(3,'Alonso','27-Jan-2022');
insert into Emp1 values(4,'Schumacher','10-Nov-2020');

select * from Emp1;

select to_char(doj,'day') from Emp1;

select empno, Name from Emp1 where to_char(doj,'fmday')='Monday';

select empno, Name from Emp1 where to_char(doj,'fmmon')='Feb';

select Name from Emp1 where doj between sysdate-30 and sysdate;


create table Train(trainno number, dod date, tod timestamp, toa timestamp);

insert into Train values(1,'02-Feb-2022','02-Feb-2022 10:30:00','02-Feb-2022 11:30:00 AM');
insert into Train values(2,'11-Jan-2022','11-Jan-2022 11:00:00','11-Jan-2022 04:00:00 PM');
insert into Train values(3,'10-Feb-2022','10-Feb-2022 08:00:00','10-Feb-2022 11:00:00 AM');
insert into Train values(4,'15-Jan-2022','15-Jan-2022 06:45:00','15-Jan-2022 08:00:00 PM');
insert into Train values(5,'04-Feb-2022','04-Feb-2022 09:00:00','04-Feb-2022 07:00:00 PM');

select* from Train;
select to_char(toa, 'hh:mm:ss') from Train;
select to_char(toa, 'hh:mm:ss PM') from Train;

select * from Train where to_char(toa, 'PM')='PM';
select * from Train where to_char(toa, 'AM')='AM';
select * from Train where tod between sysdate and sysdate +1/24;

L1-ppt

26/03/22, 13:28 - Maitreyi: Dear Students,

The Mid Semester Test (MST) is scheduled in offline mode from 28th March to 9th April, 2022 (for UG-I it is 31st March to 9th April, 2022).



The following points should please be noted regarding the conduct of MSTs:

1.      The MSTs will be subjective with 7 questions and the student will be asked to attempt any 5 questions. The MST will be of 2 hours duration with maximum marks as 35 (which will be converted to appropriate weightages as per respective evaluation schemes).

2.     Quizzes for all the courses can be scheduled along with the MST of the respective course. The maximum duration of the quiz can be 15 minutes.

3.     On the day of the examination, the quiz will be conducted before the MST i.e., the students will first appear for the quiz (which will be collected by the invigilators) and then the question paper for MST will be distributed to the students.

);

16/05/22, 20:27 - Aditya Kuthiala: Q1.

declare a number:=5; b number:=6; ans1 number; ans2 number; ans3 number; ans4 number;
procedure que1(a in number,b in number,ans1 out number,ans2 out number,ans3 out number,ans4 out number) is
begin
ans1:=a+b; ans2:=a-b; ans3:=a*b; ans4:=a/b; end; begin
que1(a,b,ans1,ans2,ans3,ans4);
dbms_output.put_line(ans1||' '||ans2||' '||ans3||' '||ans4); end;


Q2.

declare eid number:=2; bs number:=10000;
procedure raise_salary(eid in number,bs in number) is begin
    update emp set sal=sal+bs where eno=eid;
commit; end; begin raise_salary(eid,bs);
end;

Q3.

create or replace procedure fire_employee(en in number) is begin
    delete from emp where eno=en; end;

declare en number:=1; begin fire_employee(en); end;


Q4.

declare
num number; function fun return number is num number; begin
select count(*) into num from emp;
return num; end; begin num:=fun(); dbms_output.put_line(num);
end;


Q5.

create function addition(a in number,b in number) return number is ans number; begin ans:=a+b; return ans;
end;

declare a number:=10; b number:=12; ans number; begin ans:=addition(10,12); dbms_output.put_line(ans); end;


Q6.

create function stored_fun return number is num number; begin
update emp set deptno=69 where job='job69';
num:=sql%rowcount; return num;
end;

declare num number; function local_fun return number is num number; begin
update emp set deptno=69 where job='job69';
num:=sql%rowcount; return num; end;
begin num:=stored_fun(); dbms_output.put_line(num); num:=local_fun(); dbms_output.put_line(num);
end;

Q7.

create or replace trigger uppercase before insert or update of ename on emp for each row begin
:new.ename:=upper(:new.ename);
end;


Q8.

create or replace trigger show after update of ename on emp for each row begin
dbms_output.put_line('old name ='||:old.ename||' new name ='||:new.ename); end;


Q9.

create or replace trigger no_operation before insert or update or delete on emp begin
if(lower(to_char(sysdate,'day'))='sunday') then
    raise_application_error(-20000,'cannot perform operations on this table on sunday'); end if; end;

22/08/22, 11:22 - Soumil Jainer: #Q1-a
arr=c(rep('gold',20),rep('silver',30),rep('bronze',50))

#b

#Q2
# a) having same birthday
k = 2  # number of people in room
p = numeric(k)
for (i in 1:k)      {
  q = 1 - (0:(i - 1))/365
  p[i] = 1 - prod(q)  }
prob = p[k]
print(prob)

# b)

M=365
for (j in 1:M){
  k = j
  p <- numeric(k)
  for (i in 1:k)      {
    q <- 1 - (0:(i - 1))/365
    p[i] <- 1 - prod(q)  }
  prob <- p[k]

  if(prob>0.5){
    break
  }
}
print(prob)
print(k)

#Q3
c=0.4
r=0.20

27/08/22, 15:22 - Soumil Jainer: Maximize Goodness

Problem Description

You are given an integer array A and an integer B. You need to divide the array into B subarrays Le each element should belong to exactly 1 subarray The goodness of A is equal to the sum of the goodness of all its subarrays where the goodness of subarray A[...] is equal to A[I] | A[I+1]||A[r] where is Bitwise OR operator.

Q1

Return the maximum possible goodness of A if you divide it into B subarrays optimally.

Q2

Q3

Problem Constraints

1 <= |A| <= 10³

1 <= Ali] <= 230 1 BIA

Q4

The first argument is an integer array A and the second argument is an integer B

Output Format

27/08/22, 15:23 - Soumil Jainer: Walter White is trying to expand his business by making his product purer. He and Pinkman decided to add some new ingredients for cooking. While doing calculations, he came across one mysterious polynomial P(x).

51

The polynomial is of degree A. It is given that P(1) = P(2) = P(3) ..... = P(A) = 1. Additionally, P(A+1) = B.

Walt wants to know the value of P(A+C) for a given C

Q2

To help him out, Calculate the value of P(A+C) modulo 10*+7.

Note:

Q3

It can be proved that the given polynomial always exists and is unique.

Q4

Problem Constraints

1 <= A <= 5*105

2 <= B <= 10 1<< C <= 5*105

Input Format

The first argument is the integer A.

The second argument is the integer B. The third argument is the integer C..
27/08/22, 15:34 - Sukhnoor: <Media omitted>
27/08/22, 15:36 - Shreya Pawar: long Solution::solve(int A, vector<int> &B) {
    int Max=0;
    sort(B.begin(), B.end());
    for(int i=0; i<A-1; i++)
    {
        int min_val=*min_element(B.begin()+i, B.end());
        int nums=A-i;
        int val=nums*min_val;
        if (val>=Max)
        {
            Max=val;
        }
    }
    return Max;

}

getmode <- function(v) {
  uniqv <- unique(v)
  uniqv[which.max(tabulate(match(v, uniqv)))]
}
v <- c(2,1,2,3,1,2,3,4,1,5,5,3,2,3)
result <- getmode(v)
print(result)

#include <sys/socket.h>
#include <netdb.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <arpa/inet.h>
#include <unistd.h>
int main()
{
char str[100];
char reply[100];
int listen_fd, comm_fd;
struct sockaddr_in servaddr;
listen_fd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, 0);
bzero( &servaddr, sizeof(servaddr));
servaddr.sin_family = AF_INET;
servaddr.sin_addr.s_addr = htonl(INADDR_ANY);
servaddr.sin_port = htons(22000);
bind(listen_fd, (struct sockaddr *) &servaddr, sizeof(servaddr));
listen(listen_fd, 10);
comm_fd = accept(listen_fd, (struct sockaddr*) NULL, NULL);
while(1)
{
//comm_fd = accept(listen_fd, (struct sockaddr*) NULL, NULL);
bzero( str, 100);
bzero(reply,100);
recv(comm_fd,str,100,0);
printf("FROM CLIENT- %s",str);
printf("FROM SERVER:-");
fgets(reply,100,stdin);
send(comm_fd,reply,strlen(reply),0);

}
}

char recvline[100];

bzero(&servaddr,sizeof( servaddr));
servaddr.sin_family=AF_INET;
servaddr.sin_port=htons(22000);

{
bzero( sendline, 100);
bzero( recvline, 100);

}

07/09/22, 17:26 - Sukhnoor: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <sys/socket.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#include <netinet/in.h>
#include <arpa/inet.h>
char* count_length(int len){
	char ans[30];
	int i=0;
	while(len!=0){
		int temp=i%10;
		ans[i]='0'+temp;
		len/=10;
	}
	return ans;
}
int main(int argc, char **argv) {

	if (argc != 2) {
		printf("Usage: %s <port>\n", argv[0]);
		exit(0);
	}

	char *ip = "127.0.0.1";
	int port = atoi(argv[1]);

	int sockfd;
	struct sockaddr_in server_addr, client_addr;
	char buffer[1024];
	socklen_t addr_size;
	int n;

	sockfd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_DGRAM, 0);
	if (sockfd < 0) {
		perror("[-]socket error");
		exit(1);
	}

	memset(&server_addr, '\0', sizeof(server_addr));
	server_addr.sin_family = AF_INET;
	server_addr.sin_port = htons(port);
	server_addr.sin_addr.s_addr = inet_addr(ip);

	n = bind(sockfd, (struct sockaddr*)&server_addr, sizeof(server_addr));
	if (n < 0) {
		perror("[-]bind error");
		exit(1);
	}
	while (1) {
		bzero(buffer, 1024);
		addr_size = sizeof(client_addr);
		recvfrom(sockfd, buffer, 1024, 0, (struct sockaddr*)&client_addr, &addr_size);
		printf("From client --> %s\n", buffer);
		char length[30];
		int len=strlen(buffer);
		sprintf(length,"%d",len-1);
		sendto(sockfd, length, sizeof(length), 0, (struct sockaddr*)&client_addr, sizeof(client_addr));
	}

	return 0;
}

Client
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <sys/socket.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#include <netinet/in.h>
#include <arpa/inet.h>

int main(int argc, char **argv) {

	if (argc != 2) {
		printf("Usage: %s <port>\n", argv[0]);
		exit(0);
	}

	char *ip = "127.0.0.1";
	int port = atoi(argv[1]);

	int sockfd;
	struct sockaddr_in addr;
	char buffer[1024];
	socklen_t addr_size;

	sockfd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_DGRAM, 0);
	memset(&addr, '\0', sizeof(addr));
	addr.sin_family = AF_INET;
	addr.sin_port = htons(port);
	addr.sin_addr.s_addr = inet_addr(ip);

	while (1) {
		bzero(buffer, 1024);
		fgets(buffer, 1024, stdin);
		sendto(sockfd, buffer, 1024, 0, (struct sockaddr*)&addr, sizeof(addr));
		bzero(buffer, 1024);
		addr_size = sizeof(addr);
		recvfrom(sockfd, buffer, 1024, 0, (struct sockaddr*)&addr, &addr_size);
		printf("From server --> : %s\n", buffer);
	}

	return 0;
}
07/09/22, 17:47 - Shreya Pawar: #include <netdb.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <sys/socket.h>
#define MAX 80
#define PORT 2200
#define SA struct sockaddr
void func(int sockfd)
{
	char buff[MAX];
	char rbuff[4*MAX];

	for (;;) {
		bzero(buff, sizeof(buff));
		bzero(rbuff, sizeof(rbuff));
		printf("Enter the string1: ");

		scanf("%s",buff);
		write(sockfd, buff, sizeof(buff));
		printf("Enter the string2: ");

		bzero(buff, sizeof(buff));


		scanf("%s",buff);
		write(sockfd, buff, sizeof(buff));


		read(sockfd, rbuff, sizeof(rbuff));
		printf("Concatinated strings from Server : %s\n", rbuff);

	}
}

int main()
{
	int sockfd, connfd;
	struct sockaddr_in servaddr, cli;

	// socket create and verification
	sockfd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, 0);
	if (sockfd == -1) {
		printf("socket creation failed...\n");
		exit(0);
	}
	else
		printf("Socket successfully created..\n");
	bzero(&servaddr, sizeof(servaddr));

	// assign IP, PORT
	servaddr.sin_family = AF_INET;
	servaddr.sin_addr.s_addr = inet_addr("127.0.0.1");
	servaddr.sin_port = htons(PORT);

	// connect the client socket to server socket
	if (connect(sockfd, (SA*)&servaddr, sizeof(servaddr)) != 0) {
		printf("connection with the server failed...\n");
		exit(0);
	}
	else
		printf("connected to the server..\n");

	// function for chat
	func(sockfd);

	// close the socket
	close(sockfd);
}

07/09/22, 17:48 - Shreya Pawar: #include <stdio.h>
#include <netdb.h>
#include <netinet/in.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <sys/socket.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#define MAX 80
#define PORT 2200
#define SA struct sockaddr

void func(int connfd)
{
	char buff1[4*MAX];
	char buff2[MAX];

	for (;;) {
		bzero(buff1, sizeof(buff1));
		bzero(buff2, sizeof(buff2));

		// read the message1 from client and copy it in buffer
		read(connfd, buff1, sizeof(buff1));
		printf("String1:%s\n",buff1);
		// read the message2 from client and copy it in buffer
		read(connfd,buff2,sizeof(buff2));
		printf("String2:%s\n",buff2);
		strcat(strcat(buff1," "),buff2);
		printf("Sending To Client %s\n",buff1);
		// print buffer which contains the client contents
		// and send that buffer to client
		write(connfd, buff1, sizeof(buff1));

}

int main()
{
	int sockfd, connfd, len;
	struct sockaddr_in servaddr, cli;

	sockfd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, 0);
	if (sockfd == -1) {
		printf("socket creation failed...\n");
		exit(0);
	}
	else
		printf("Socket successfully created..\n");
	bzero(&servaddr, sizeof(servaddr));
	// assign IP, PORT
	servaddr.sin_family = AF_INET;
	servaddr.sin_addr.s_addr = htonl(INADDR_ANY);
	servaddr.sin_port = htons(PORT);
	// Binding newly created socket to given IP and verification
	if ((bind(sockfd, (SA*)&servaddr, sizeof(servaddr))) != 0) {
		printf("socket bind failed...\n");
		exit(0);
	}
	else
		printf("Socket successfully binded..\n");

	// Now server is ready to listen and verification
	if ((listen(sockfd, 5)) != 0) {
		printf("Listen failed...\n");
		exit(0);
	}
	else
		printf("Server listening..\n");
	len = sizeof(cli);

	// Accept the data packet from client and verification
	connfd = accept(sockfd, (SA*)&cli, &len);
	if (connfd < 0) {
		printf("server accept failed...\n");
		exit(0);
	}
	else
		printf("server accept the client...\n");

	// Function for chatting between client and server
	func(connfd);

	// After chatting close the socket
	close(sockfd);
}

Expert Answer
General Guidance
The answer provided below has been developed in a clear step by step manner.
Step: 1
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#include <sys/socket.h>
#include <netinet/in.h>
#include <arpa/inet.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <pthread.h>
#include <netdb.h>
#define MAX 1024
int sockfd;

// Function to display error
void error(const char *msg)
{
    perror(msg);
    exit(1);
}

// Function to read file
int get_file_size(int fd)
{
    struct stat stat_buf;
    fstat(fd, &stat_buf);
    return (int) stat_buf.st_size;
}

void *read_write(void *arg)
{
    int sockfd = *((int *)arg);
    int fd, n;
    int recv_fd;
    char fname[MAX];
    char file_size[MAX];
    char buf[MAX];
    char *filedata;

    // Get the file name from client
    read(sockfd, fname, MAX);

    // Open the requested file
    fd = open(fname, O_RDONLY);

    // Read file into a buffer
    filedata = (char *)malloc(sizeof(char) * get_file_size(fd));
    recv(sockfd, filedata, get_file_size(fd), 0);

    // Write the file contents back to client
    write(sockfd, filedata, get_file_size(fd));
    close(sockfd);
}

int main(int argc, char *argv[])
{
    if (argc < 2)
    {
        fprintf(stderr,"ERROR, no port provided\n");
        exit(1);
    }
    int sockfd, newsockfd, portno, n;
    struct sockaddr_in serv_addr;
    struct sockaddr_in cli_addr;
    socklen_t clilen;

    // Create a socket
    sockfd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, 0);
    if (sockfd < 0)
    {
        error("ERROR opening socket");
    }

    // Clear serv_addr
    bzero((char *) &serv_addr, sizeof(serv_addr));

    // Get portno from command line
    portno = atoi(argv[1]);

    // Fill serv_addr
    serv_addr.sin_family = AF_INET;
    serv_addr.sin_addr.s_addr = INADDR_ANY;
    serv_addr.sin_port = htons(portno);

    // Bind the host address
    if (bind(sockfd, (struct sockaddr *) &serv_addr, sizeof(serv_addr)) < 0)
    {
        error("ERROR on binding");
    }

    // Start listening for the clients
    listen(sockfd, 5);
    clilen = sizeof(cli_addr);

    // Accept actual connection from the client
    newsockfd = accept(sockfd, (struct sockaddr *)&cli_addr, &clilen);

    if (newsockfd < 0)
    {
        error("ERROR on accept");
    }

    pthread_t tid;
    int err = pthread_create(&tid, NULL, &read_write, (void *)&newsockfd);
    if (err != 0)
    {
        printf("\ncan't create thread :[%s]", strerror(err));
    }
    pthread_join(tid, NULL);
    close(newsockfd);
    close(sockfd);

    return 0;
}




Explanation:
Explanation:
Assuming that you want a multi-threaded HTTP server which can serve multiple clients concurrently, you can use the pthread library to create separate threads for each client.

Step: 2
Explanation:

In the main function, you will first create a socket and bind it to a port number. Then you will start listening for incoming connections. When a client connects, you will accept the connection and create a new thread. This thread will be responsible for serving the client.
The read_write function is the thread function. It takes the socket file descriptor as an argument. This function will read the file name from the client. Then it will open the file and read its contents into a buffer. Finally, it will write the contents of the buffer back to the client.
You can compile the above code using the gcc compiler as follows:
$ gcc -o server server.c -lpthread
To run the server, you can specify the port number as an argument as follows:
$ ./server 8080
This will start the server on port 8080. You can now connect to the server using a web browser.

15/10/22, 09:20 - Sukhnoor: #include <sys/types.h>
#include <sys/socket.h>
#include <netdb.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include<string.h>
int main(int argc,char **argv)
{
int sockfd,n;
char sendline[100];
char recvline[100];
struct sockaddr_in servaddr;
int server_struct_length=sizeof(servaddr);
sockfd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_DGRAM, 0);
int broadcastEnable=1;
int ret=setsockopt(sockfd, SOL_SOCKET, SO_BROADCAST, &broadcastEnable, sizeof(broadcastEnable));
//sockfd=socket(AF_INET,SOCK_DGRAM,IPPROTO_UDP);

{
